+0000","feedId":21,"bgimg":"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/arc-106-18739_r2_12f8915f-e1626270910217-700x302.jpeg","linkMd5":"877e0126667b221407f23131ac1ca5d4","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn29@2020_5/2021/07/14/17-33-39-131_dfd8e2da80d07ba1.webp","destWidth":700,"destHeight":302,"sourceBytes":24461,"destBytes":11900,"author":"Joshua Meyer","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/arc-106-18739_r2_12f8915f-e1626270910217-700x302.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn29@2020_5/2021/07/14/17-33-39-131_dfd8e2da80d07ba1.webp","https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Season-1-Finale-Miss-Minutes-700x300.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn83@2020_6/2021/07/14/17-33-46-702_6c15f32c7c38f450.webp","https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Season-1-Finale-Jonathan-Majors-700x300.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn88@2020_2/2021/07/14/17-33-46-706_1e6e3d72c93f295e.webp","https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Season-1-Finale-Kang-Statue-700x300.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn80@2020_5/2021/07/14/17-33-47-060_782251b536541b1a.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn40@2020_4/2021/07/14/17-33-46-881_9a442e8760d02cd4.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?i=Uf01YnVnE3k:XBEjvO8HWOI:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn92@2020_6/2021/07/14/17-33-46-343_b59842e9a83efb06.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?d=I9og5sOYxJI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn92@2020_6/2021/07/14/17-33-47-600_879c5505f034c3d2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?i=Uf01YnVnE3k:XBEjvO8HWOI:EGzC5_Ws_ZE":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn56@2020_6/2021/07/14/17-33-47-475_328d84c6a83c0914.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/slashfilm/~4/Uf01YnVnE3k":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn91@2020_2/2021/07/14/17-33-46-665_a1ebe3ec7b848afc.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1626284004433},{"createdTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:24","updatedTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:24","title":"‘Loki’ Finale Reveals Who’s Behind the TVA Curtain – and That Answer Brings Up a ‘Multiverse’ of Questions","link":"https://www.slashfilm.com/?p=683655","description":"<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-683657 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/cit1020_106_comp_v005_afa9d2b6-700x294.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"294\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/cit1020_106_comp_v005_afa9d2b6.jpeg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/cit1020_106_comp_v005_afa9d2b6-360x151.jpeg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>The first season of <strong><em>Loki</em></strong> is done. We got some answers mixed with exposition, a lot of drama with some tears, and a lot of dangling threads (or branches, if you like) for Marvel to pull on in <em><strong>Doctor Strange in the </strong></em><strong><em>Multiverse of Madness</em></strong> and/or season 2 of the Disney+ show.</p>\n<p>There are <em>so</em> many loose threads and exposition in this finale, that it really isn’t a finale at all.  In many ways, the last third of the episode is more like a prologue for <em>Multiverse of Madness</em> and is tonally tinged with a <em>Doctor Strange</em> feel.</p>\n<p>Whether that’s a good thing…different Variants can have different thoughts on that. For me, I like that interconnectedness. But I’m also someone who likes the MCU so much that I <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/marvel-marathon-diary/\">spent 30+ hours in an old theater for a Marvel movie marathon</a>. Others’ mileage may vary. Read on for a spoiler-full breakdown of the latest episode.</p>\n<p><em>Warning!</em> <em><strong>Spoilers</strong> abound below for the sixth episode of Disney+’s </em>Loki<em>, “<strong>For All Time. Always.”</strong></em></p>\n<p><span id=\"more-683655\"></span></p>\n<h2><strong>There Are Multiverses Out There Just Waiting to Fight Each Other </strong></h2>\n<p>This episode is all about the multiverses. What are they? Why do they matter? Who’s behind it all?  “For All Time. Always.” answers that, and it all starts with a new Marvel opening banner. The Marvel sequence looks similar at first. Then, however, we hear other Avengers saying some of their favorite catchphrases (We hear Steve Rodgers say “I could do this all day,” for example).</p>\n<p>And then things get trippy. We zoom in and out of space and time in a very <em>Doctor Strange</em>-esque manner as quotes from IRL folks like Maya Angelou join the voiceover. Things eventually coalesce into a cosmic ring (AKA The Sacred Timeline) around The Citadel in The Void At The End of Time, and we’re back with our two Lokis (<strong>Tom Hiddleston </strong>and <strong>Sophia Di Martino</strong>).</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-683658 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/rns1220_106_comp_v008_6a60bcbd-700x293.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"293\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/rns1220_106_comp_v008_6a60bcbd.jpeg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/rns1220_106_comp_v008_6a60bcbd-360x151.jpeg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<h2><strong>It Was Miss Minutes All Along</strong></h2>\n<p>Okay, not really. We <em>do</em> see the TVA’s animated clock (voiced by <strong>Tara Strong</strong>) when Sylvie and Loki walk into the Citadel. And in quest-like fashion, tempts our two anti-heroes with whatever their hearts’ desire.</p>\n<p>Miss Minutes also clues us in that there’s one being behind everything, who she ominously calls He Who Remains. (It’s also here where MCU fans start screaming, “It’s Kang the Conqueror!” at their TVs.)</p>\n<p>Sylvie and Loki decline the offer, concluding (correctly, I’d guess) that it was a lie. Or maybe it was a “test” they had to pass? Just like the kids in <em>Willy Wonka</em> went through to see who could take over Wonka’s factory?</p>\n<p>There’s a lot of Willy Wonka vibes going on in this episode. (And Wizard of Oz, but we’ve seen that already in the show.) And that brings us to the MCU’s version of Wonka: He Who Remains, played by <strong>Jonathan Majors</strong>. While the show doesn’t call him Kang the Conqueror, that’s who he is! We know this not only because news of <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/ant-man-3-villain/\">Majors’ casting</a> has been out for months now, but because we get his character’s entire origin story.</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-683640\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Season-1-Finale-Jonathan-Majors-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Season-1-Finale-Jonathan-Majors-700x300.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Season-1-Finale-Jonathan-Majors-360x154.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Season-1-Finale-Jonathan-Majors-768x329.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<h2><strong>Let the Exposition Flow</strong></h2>\n<p>Kang (I’m going to call him that because He Who Remains is too pretentious for me, plus it takes too long to type) is a quirky guy. This version of him anyway. It turns out that he’s a human from the 31st century who discovered how to travel between multiverses. Other versions of him figured it out as well, and for a while they all got along.</p>\n<p>And then they didn’t! Some versions of Kang weren’t so nice…they were conquerors even. (In my headcanon, however, one Kang Variant <em>is</em> Willy Wonka. Don’t tell me I’m wrong, let me live with this fictional fiction.) The Kangs started fighting, and we got the Multiversal Wars.</p>\n<p>The Kang talking to Sylvie and Loki explains this all in his wacked out avuncular way (he also has little CGI figurines to help tell the tale), and then he offers the two a golden ticket. <em>They</em> can take over Kang’s job and stave off another Multiversal War from happening. If they did, they’d also have complete power over time and space, something that’d be appealing to many a Loki.</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-683659 size-medium\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/arc-106-18739_r2_12f8915f-e1626270910217-700x302.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"302\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/arc-106-18739_r2_12f8915f-e1626270910217.jpeg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/arc-106-18739_r2_12f8915f-e1626270910217-360x155.jpeg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<h2><strong>&#8220;You Can’t Trust and I Can’t Be Trusted&#8221;</strong></h2>\n<p>Kang lays this all out for Sylvie and Loki just as The Void crosses some threshold and he no longer knows what’s going to happen next. It’s here where we get the only major emotional moment of the episode (except for a short one between <strong>Gugu Mbatha-Raw</strong>&#8216;s Ravonna and <strong>Owen Wilson</strong>&#8216;s Mobius).</p>\n<p>This scene <em>is</em> moving — Di Martino and Hiddleston deftly convey how they care for each other, even if their respective Loki traits threaten to create a rift between them.</p>\n<p>It’s also not enough for me — so much of the series up to this point has been about these two characters and how they’ve grown and found a connection with each other. This finale veers away from that, something that’s arguably necessary given it has to set up whatever is coming in <em>Multiverse of Madness</em>. And the ultimate rift between the two — Sylvie sends Loki back to the TVA and kills Kang — also sets up good character fodder for the second season, so there’s that.</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-683635\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Finale-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Finale-700x300.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Finale-360x154.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Loki-Finale-768x329.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<h2><strong>Loki? What’s a Loki?</strong></h2>\n<p>After Sylvie successfully and anti-climatically kills Kang, the multiverse falls into madness! Just as this version of Kang warned, millions of branches pop up, causing million of versions of himself to wreak havoc across space and time.</p>\n<p>Back at the TVA, Loki desperately tries to find his friends and tell him what’s happened. He finds Mobius and B-15 (<strong>Wunmi Mosaku</strong>) and frantically explains everything. Mobius and B-15, however, give him blank stares: they have no idea who Loki is. That means that they not only don’t know this version of Loki, but any of the other Variants.</p>\n<p>The scene then cuts to one of the TVA’s monolith statues. The image isn’t one of the fake Time-Keepers — it’s Kang himself. The TVA’s timeline has veered off course, and only Loki, it seems, remembers how things were.</p>\n<p>That’s not <em>entirely</em> true. Sylvie likely still knows what’s up. And then Ravonna is also out there somewhere trying to “find free will” after she spared Mobius’ life and took a time portal to somewhere/when unknown, though my guess is it’s someplace with a less-evil version of Kang. (Side note: Ravonna being a school principal on Earth fits <em>perfectly</em> with her character.)</p>\n<p>And there we leave it! Lots of questions, but also the promise of a season 2 in a brief post-credit moment. Over six episodes, <em>Loki</em> accomplished a lot, and I’m not just talking about making a push for a Josta soda comeback.</p>\n<p>We got to delve deep into one of Marvel’s bad/not-so-great guys, and we also got the joy that is <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/alligator-loki/\">Alligator Loki</a> and <strong>Richard E. Grant</strong> in a Classic Loki suit. What a vast place the MCU is, and what characters live within it. I can’t wait to see more of them as Phase 4 rolls out.<strong> </strong></p>\n<p>All six episodes of the first season of <em>Loki</em> are now streaming on Disney+.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/loki-finale-review/\">&#8216;Loki&#8217; Finale Reveals Who&#8217;s Behind the TVA Curtain – and That Answer Brings Up a &#8216;Multiverse&#8217; of Questions</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com\">/Film</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a 01:33:24","updatedTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:24","title":"Nicolas Cage Won’t be Adding Joe Exotic to His Roster of Memeable Roles as ‘Tiger King’ Series Gets Shelved","link":"https://www.slashfilm.com/?p=683733","description":"<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-616032 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Nicolas-Cage-Tiger-King-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"Nicolas Cage Tiger King\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Nicolas-Cage-Tiger-King.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Nicolas-Cage-Tiger-King-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>You win some and you lose some and, in this case, we&#8217;re very much chalking this up to a win. For those of us who die on the hill that <strong>Nicolas Cage</strong> is an immensely talented actor (watch <em><strong>Leaving Las Vegas</strong></em>, to remind yourselves!) whose almost inhuman energy should not be wasted, we&#8217;re not <em>too</em> sad to report that Cage won&#8217;t be joining Amazon&#8217;s Joe Exotic series <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/nicolas-cage-tiger-king/\">as previously reported</a>.</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-683733\"></span></p>\n<p>According to <a href=\"https://variety.com/2021/film/news/nicolas-cage-joe-exotic-amazon-series-1235019225/\">Variety</a>, the project has been placed on the shelf and may be shopped around to other outlets. Meanwhile, Cage himself broke the news that he is no longer attached to the role, saying:</p>\n<blockquote><p>&#8220;We should clear the record. I read two excellent scripts, which I did think were excellent, but I think Amazon ultimately felt that it was material that had become past tense because it took so long for it come together. They felt at one point that it was lightning in a bottle, but that point has since faded into the distance and it’s no longer relevant.&#8221;</p></blockquote>\n<p>That makes a lot of sense and, honestly, it&#8217;s kind of refreshing to hear an actor just come out and say that a once-exciting idea was little more than a momentary fad. Obviously capitalizing on Netflix&#8217;s flash-in-the-pan success with their <em><strong>Tiger King</strong></em> documentary, this project was meant to focus on the eccentric man at the center of the wildly popular show, as opposed to its revolving door of unconventional side characters.</p>\n<p>On the surface, at least, I suppose Cage made for a decently obvious casting choice for the wild zookeeper. But to me, it always seemed a poor fit to me and beneath the actor, somehow. This was always a project that needed Nicolas Cage more than Nicolas Cage needed it.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-512354 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/mandy-box-office-700x321.jpg\" alt=\"mandy box office\" width=\"700\" height=\"321\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/mandy-box-office-700x321.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/mandy-box-office-360x165.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/mandy-box-office-768x352.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/mandy-box-office.jpg 948w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<h2>The Man, The Myth, The Cage</h2>\n<p>But not to worry, folks, because the Cage train simply does not stop. Lest we forget that Cage will be <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/unbearable-weight-of-massive-talent/\">starring as himself in <em><strong>The Unbearable Weight of Massive Talent</strong></em></a>, a hilariously meta-sounding movie that features a fictionalized Nicolas Cage getting mixed up with the CIA, drug cartels, and who even knows what else. Even more excitingly, the enigma of an actor is drawing praise for his turn in <em><strong>Pig</strong></em>, the surprisingly thoughtful drama in which he plays a loner on the relentless search for his kidnapped pig. <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/pig-review/\">Our own Chris Evangelista raves</a> about Cage&#8217;s performance, complimenting his &#8220;subtle grace that is bound to shock folks.&#8221;</p>\n<p>Cage Cinema is alive and well, which we absolutely love to see.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/nicolas-cage-tiger-king-series-canceled/\">Nicolas Cage Won&#8217;t be Adding Joe Exotic to His Roster of Memeable Roles as &#8216;Tiger King&#8217; Series Gets Shelved</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com\">/Film</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a +0000","feedId":21,"bgimg":"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Nicolas-Cage-Tiger-King-700x300.jpg","linkMd5":"fbf805ca7aee9fee22bd5711d92e7fdb","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn37@2020_6/2021/07/14/17-33-39-163_cae7410d7a8e9666.webp","destWidth":700,"destHeight":300,"sourceBytes":55935,"destBytes":41564,"author":"Jeremy src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot1-frontpage-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"NECA Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles in Disguise Action Figures\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot1-frontpage.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot1-frontpage-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>NECA has an ongoing deal that makes Target the exclusive retailer for action figures inspired by the <strong><em>Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles</em></strong> animated series. That has made many of the <em>TMNT</em> action figures rather tough for collectors to snag. Thankfully, NECA has been able to offer pre-orders of <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-metalhead-action-figure/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">some of the hard-to-find animated figures</a> through their own online shop, and the pre-order treatment is finally being given to one of the coveted sets featuring all four of the heroes in a half-shell: Turtles in Disguise.<span id=\"more-683612\"></span></p>\n\n<a href='https://www.slashfilm.com/neca-teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-in-disguise-action-figures/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot1/'><img width=\"360\" height=\"240\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot1-360x240.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"NECA Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles in Disguise Action Figures\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot1-360x240.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot1.jpg 700w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 360px) 100vw, 360px\" /></a>\n<a href='https://www.slashfilm.com/neca-teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-in-disguise-action-figures/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot2/'><img width=\"360\" height=\"240\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot2-360x240.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"NECA Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles in Disguise Action Figures\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot2-360x240.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-promoshot2.jpg 700w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 360px) 100vw, 360px\" /></a>\n\n<h2>NECA Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles in Disguise Action Figures</h2>\n<p>Inspired by the second episode of the third season of the <em>Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles</em> animated series, this action figure four-pack features the turtles in their horrifying human disguises given to them by April O&#8217;Neil. Along with the creepy human masks, the turtles also put on hats, pants, and trench coats. Surely that will be enough to distract people from the fact that they all have the exact same face.</p>\n\n<a href='https://www.slashfilm.com/neca-teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-in-disguise-action-figures/tmnt-disguise-4pack-boxfront/'><img width=\"360\" height=\"360\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-boxfront-360x360.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"NECA Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles in Disguise Action Figures\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-boxfront-360x360.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-boxfront.jpg 700w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 360px) 100vw, 360px\" /></a>\n<a href='https://www.slashfilm.com/neca-teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles-in-disguise-action-figures/tmnt-disguise-4pack-boxopen/'><img width=\"360\" height=\"360\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-boxopen-360x360.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"NECA Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles in Disguise Action Figures\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-boxopen-360x360.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-boxopen.jpg 700w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 360px) 100vw, 360px\" /></a>\n\n<p>Along with the horrifying disguises, the NECA <em>Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles</em> in disguise action figures also come with some fun accessories, such as a boombox, a skateboard, a pigeon, a couple pizzas (and a slice), a &#8220;weird&#8221; baseball cap, and <em>The Hare and the Tortoise</em> book. Plus, since they&#8217;re the Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles, they also have their traditional weapons, as well as interchangeable hands and heads for various poses.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-683618 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-everything-700x726.jpg\" alt=\"NECA Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles in Disguise Action Figures\" width=\"700\" height=\"726\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-everything.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/tmnt-disguise-4pack-everything-360x373.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>The NECA<em> Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles</em> in disguise action figures were $99.99 on Target shelves, so they&#8217;ll presumably be around the same price when they go on sale at the <a href=\"https://thenecastore.com/collections/teenage-mutant-ninja-turtles\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">NECA online store</a> starting today (<strong>July 14</strong>) at 11:00 A.M. ET. But they will only be available for two weeks, so don&#8217;t wait!</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" 33-46-760_4c485153397a2a57.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1626284004433},{"createdTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:24","updatedTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:24","title":"Indie Giant A24 Recently Entertained a Potential $3 Billion Dollar Sale","link":"https://www.slashfilm.com/?p=683557","description":"<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-277950 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/a24-logo-700x298.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"298\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/a24-logo.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/a24-logo-360x153.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>In the Netflix era, more and more movies, particularly mid-budget dramas, have shifted to streaming services. And in an effort to compete with each other and woo subscribers, those services have been looking to acquire companies that would help them expand their libraries. These are the circumstances under which indie studio <strong>A24</strong> may be looking to broker a sale.</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-683557\"></span></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://variety.com/2021/film/news/inside-a24-billion-dollar-sale-1235018988/\">Variety</a> reports that A24 has been testing the market for a potential sale, &#8220;floating an asking price of between $2.5 billion to $3 billion.&#8221; If that seems like a steep amount, consider the climate, where MGM recently sold to Amazon <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/amazon-buys-mgm/\">for $8.6 billion</a>, and where smaller banners like Reese Witherspoon&#8217;s Hello Sunshine is said to be <a href=\"https://www.wsj.com/articles/reese-witherspoons-media-company-hello-sunshine-is-exploring-a-sale-11625605587\">valued at $1 billion</a>.</p>\n<p>By comparison, when Disney <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/disney-buys-lucasfilm-new-star-wars-film-2015/\">bought Lucasfilm in 2012</a>, it paid $4 billion for the studio, which now seems like a lowball figure. The moviegoing terrain has changed considerably since then, with the coronavirus shuttering theaters and bringing the industry closer to the feared &#8220;implosion&#8221; that George Lucas and Steven Spielberg <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/steven-spielberg-and-george-lucas-predict-hollywood-implosion-look-towards-tv/\">spoke of back in 2013</a>. With the pandemic-best box office <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/black-widow-box-office-pandemic-record/\">success of <em>Black Widow</em></a>, there&#8217;s every sign now that things are rebounding, but for the time being, at least, that movie and most other new releases are still following the simultaneous theatrical and digital <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/warner-bros-2021/\">release strategy of Warner Bros.</a></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-638085 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/On-the-Rocks-film-still-Sofia-Coppola-1-1600x900-c-default-e1600949430660-700x320.jpeg\" alt=\"on the rocks review\" width=\"700\" height=\"320\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/On-the-Rocks-film-still-Sofia-Coppola-1-1600x900-c-default-e1600949430660-700x320.jpeg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/On-the-Rocks-film-still-Sofia-Coppola-1-1600x900-c-default-e1600949430660-360x165.jpeg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/On-the-Rocks-film-still-Sofia-Coppola-1-1600x900-c-default-e1600949430660-768x351.jpeg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/On-the-Rocks-film-still-Sofia-Coppola-1-1600x900-c-default-e1600949430660.jpeg 1600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<h2>What Makes A24 Unique</h2>\n<p>We recently talked about the A24 brand <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/lamb-trailer-noomi-rapace/\">in relation to horror</a>. The studio is known for its innovative marketing, like binding the 150-tweet thread that inspired <em>Zola</em> into a <a href=\"https://shop.a24films.com/products/the-story-by-aziah-king\">clothbound hardcover</a>. It&#8217;s also known for its spooky trailers, some of which have been slightly misleading, setting up audiences (and disgruntled CinemaScore responders) <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/it-comes-at-night-trailer/\">with monster-movie expectations</a>, when they were really about to experience <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/it-comes-at-night-misleading-trailer/\">a slow-burn psychodrama</a>. We should have known what to expect by the time <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/hereditary-trailer/\"><em>Hereditary</em></a> and <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/midsommar-trailer-new/\"><em>Midsommar</em></a> rolled around, but alas.</p>\n<p>Of course, A24 isn&#8217;t only an indie-horror boutique. It&#8217;s also responsible for &#8220;sci-fi caviar&#8221; (as iTunes likes to package it) such as <em>Ex Machina</em>, <em>High Life</em>, and <em>Under the Skin</em>. In addition, the studio has received dozens of Oscar nominations for films like <em>Room </em>and a big Best Picture win in 2018 with <em>Moonlight</em>.</p>\n<p>Per Variety, the move to potentially sell is one that has been going on under the radar for the last year and a half, yet the trade cites sources within the studio that say A24 is now &#8220;focused on expansion and is not prioritizing a sale.&#8221; We often hear rumblings of this kind right before the deals go through, so if one does happen soon, what would A24 look like under a major media company? Would it get swallowed up or might it prosper in new ways?</p>\n<p>The studio already has an <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/apple-a24-deal/\">existing deal</a> with Apple, which has debuted Sofia Coppola&#8217;s <em>On the Rocks</em> and other films as Apple TV+ exclusives. However, they&#8217;ve reportedly &#8220;passed on numerous titles&#8221; that A24 was floating, so that may be a wash.</p>\n<p>Becoming a subsidy of a larger corporation might allow A24 to reach a new audience. Alternatively, its niche appeal might get lost in the sea of subscription options and we may see the edges of a unique studio sanded off. As always with the pivot to streaming, the fear is that this is potentially one of those things where the toothpaste can&#8217;t be put back in the tube.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/a24-potential-bids/\">Indie Giant A24 Recently Entertained a Potential $3 Billion Dollar Sale</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com\">/Film</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/slashfilm?a=fV8OwmGoi_c:YPYsDj_9Aek:yIl2AUoC8zA\"><img 01:33:24","updatedTime":"2021-07-15 01:33:24","title":"Bo Burnham Was Nominated for Six Emmys for ‘Bo Burnham: Inside,’ Which is Pretty Impressive for Bo Burnham","link":"https://www.slashfilm.com/?p=683715","description":"<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-674920 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Bo-Burnham-Inside-700x300.jpg\" alt=\"Bo Burnham Inside\" width=\"700\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Bo-Burnham-Inside.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Bo-Burnham-Inside-360x154.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<p>Daddy made us some content&#8230; and now he&#8217;s nominated for six Emmy awards.</p>\n<p>Comedian <strong>Bo Burnham </strong>did the impossible with his Netflix comedy special <em><strong>Inside</strong></em><em>.</em> Our own Ben Pearson <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/the-daily-stream-theres-no-other-way-to-say-this-bo-burnham-inside-is-a-masterpiece/\">called it a masterpiece</a> and I completely agree — it&#8217;s 90 minutes of staring straight into the existential void, complete with catchy songs and some absolutely gorgeous visuals. I mean, it&#8217;s not every day that Netflix decides to actually put something of theirs <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/bo-burnham-inside-theatrical-release/\">in theaters</a>. (That&#8217;s right, at the end of this month, we can go sit inside and watch <em>Inside</em>, together!)</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-683715\"></span></p>\n<p>While it might not exactly be &#8220;healing the world with comedy,&#8221; six <a href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/2021-emmy-nominations/\">Emmy nominations</a> is nothing to sneeze at. If he wins at least five of them, he will make Emmy history for taking home the most wins in a single ceremony. (That title is currently held by <em><strong>Schitt&#8217;s Creek</strong></em>&#8216;s <strong>Dan Levy</strong>, who took home four statues in 2020.)</p>\n<p><em>Inside</em> is nominated for Outstanding Variety Special (Pre-Recorded), while Burnham himself is nominated for Outstanding Directing For a Variety Special, Outstanding Picture Editing For Variety Programing, Outstanding Music Direction, Outstanding Original Music and Lyrics, and Outstanding Writing For a Variety Special.</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-medium wp-image-675330 aligncenter\" src=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Bo-Burnham-Inside-Album-700x321.jpg\" alt=\"Bo Burnham Inside Album\" width=\"700\" height=\"321\" srcset=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Bo-Burnham-Inside-Album-700x321.jpg 700w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Bo-Burnham-Inside-Album-360x165.jpg 360w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Bo-Burnham-Inside-Album-768x352.jpg 768w, https://www.slashfilm.com/wp/wp-content/images/Bo-Burnham-Inside-Album.jpg 948w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px\" /></p>\n<h2>An Award-Worthy One-Man Show</h2>\n<p>So what makes <em>Inside </em>so impressive? Burnham did the entire thing himself, that&#8217;s what. Over the course of a year during the coronavirus pandemic, he wrote, recorded, and edited together a musical comedy special that is both heartbreaking and hilarious. The entire special takes place in the one room, and we see Burnham as he processes everything. His hair and beard grow longer, the dark circles under his eyes get darker, and we watch as a man basically has an extended existential crisis. An entire historically horrific year is compressed into 90 minutes, an experience that occasionally feels like a complete nervous breakdown.</p>\n<p>Every element of <em>Inside</em> is excellent on a technical level as well as an artistic level. Burnham manages to make the one-room location into so much more through the use of a projector, lighting, and props. It would be easy to set up a single camera and just let it roll, but he uses multiple angles and a variety of cuts to make a visually cohesive, emotionally resonant work of art. On top of the writing, cinematography, and editing, the songs are absolute bangers. There&#8217;s a reason that the album debuted at #1 on the Billboard Comedy Charts and, at the time of this writing, is sitting at #11 on the Top 200 music chart.</p>\n<p>You can check out <em>Inside</em> for yourself on Netflix or <a href=\"https://www.boburnhaminside.com/\">in theaters</a> <strong>July 22-25</strong>, and you can catch the 73rd Primetime Emmy Awards and maybe see Burnham make history on <strong>September 19</strong> on CBS and Paramount Plus.</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.slashfilm.com/bo-burnham-emmy-nominations-bo-burnham-inside/\">Bo Burnham Was Nominated for Six Emmys for &#8216;Bo Burnham: Inside,&#8217; Which is Pretty Impressive for Bo
